Their prices just went up again, so its a good $20 bucks for just a normal trim with tip.  But when you live downtown and need a cut every couple of months, its the usual spot.  Be sure to call before hand and put in your name to gauge the wait time, then you can manage your window shopping on State Street and Blender's fruit smoothie shop next door. When its summer tourist season there may be a long wait, this is not a locals only joint.</text>

< Review>
Update only to say we keep coming back here and are always happy that we did  this place is outstanding!

I just love this place! From the high quality of the seafood and the size of the portions to the staff who work there.

Not so easy to see from the street to keep aware but it does have a parking lot shared with a couple of other stores in the strip, I've seen it quite full but haven't had a problem finding a spot to park.

Look to the walls for pictures from the menu, I like choosing by look so I try new things. One of the new things is their Nachos Marinos, my favorite and what I have every other time I am there.

My father, who really appreciates hot good, ordered a dish and asked for hot - the waiter warned us that it would be hot - and it was. My father loved every minute of it! Said it was a proper hot and that it started warm but built as he ate. My dad can be picky and he was happy, I expect he'll be visiting on his own.< /Review>

CROOK  I will be updating my review regarding my experience with this place. I'd think twice about giving them my business. I dropped off one of our work vans off last week to address the check engine light. We found two codes and told Alex prior to bringing the van what the two codes were. He calls me with an estimate of $3244.00. It was actually $3359.23 when I arrived. He stated I needed a new catalytic converter and sensors replaced. I acquiesced and approved as we need to get the vehicle smogged. When I picked the vehicle up just before entering the freeway the check engine light reappeared! I turned around and took the van back and asked "why did I just pay $3400, the check engine light is on!?" . I was told Alex slipped out, I sat and waited, when he returned he plugged in the code reader and showed me a code for the DEF heater. I reminded him once again, we already told him it was on!! I left the van yet again. Alex called late the following morning and stated this repair would be $1700! I refused and told him I will pick my van up. I ubered (for the 3rd time at a cost of $105 total) to retrieve my van. He asked what I planned to do about the DEF heater, I asked AGAIN for the return of my NOX sensors he claims he replaced, after an "oh, um.... the scrap guy came and picked them up just yesterday" I reminded him I requested my old parts back! You know, PER CALIFORNIA LAW! I digress, I told him his pricing is outrageous trying to charge me ANOTHER $1700 after getting paid $3400, my God I can buy a used car!!! I told him the OEM DEF filter online is $600 MAX, the def tank which I have removed before is held in with 4 bolts, it's a 45minute job!! Who the hell makes $1864 an hour!!! Apparently Alex. I know he gets them even cheaper. He goes on to feed me some line about "If it doesn't come in a Mercedes box" You are full of sh*t! Mercedes doesn't make the DEF heater, many of the OEM parts are Bosch. He claimed he would show me his "invoice" which I had already had it with my intelligence being insulted. I know how this works, and I am not interested in seeing a fake invoice which reflects a catalog price or suggested retail price. When I asked for the nox sensors they claim they replaced $990 plus tax plus installation alex replied "oh, uh, the scrap guy picked them up". You scrapped MY parts, who gave you permission to scrap my parts. I reminded Alex I stated I wanted them back, you know, PER CALIFORNIA LAW! Per California Automotive Repair act 1974 The shop is required by law to return the parts to you only if you ask for them before the work is done.  Perhaps this is why Anthony quit working here</Review>

<Text>I really liked this place!
The only other place I've been to or seen a Rabbit Rabbit was in Taiwan.

They have a nice selection of fresh drink options that range from traditional to more unique Asian flavours.

I got the Japanese buckwheat milk tea with real taro in the bottom, and it was very filling and tasty!
If I were ever in the area I would go here again.

They're located at a Kiosk on the top floor of the Westfield mall, and there always seemed to be a small line.</Text>< name>
